35a4(mdo sde2): thos kyi dge 'dun de ni/ tshul khrims phun gsum tshogs pa/ ting nge 'dzin phun sum tshogs pa/ shes rab phun sum tshogs pa/ rnam par grol ba phun gsum tshogs
35a5(mdo sde2): ga rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba'i phun sum tshogs pa/ kun tu sbyin pa'i 'os su gyur pa/ thal mo sbyar ba'i 'os su gyur pa/ phyag bya ba'i 'os su gyur pa/

40a6(mdo sde2): dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po thams cad kyang sngon ral pa can thams cad kyang dgra bcom pa/ zag pa zad pa/ bya ba byas pa/ byed pa byas pa/

40a8(mdo sde2): cig du yul ma ga d+har yul rgyu zhing gshegs pa na/ maM ga d+ha ba rnams kyi mchod rten rab brtan smyug ma'i nags khrod ga la ba der gshegs te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das
40b1(mdo sde2): rab brtan du byon nas/ ma ga d+ha pa rnams kyi mchod rten rab brtan gyi smyug ma'i nags khrod na bzhags so// yul ma ga d+ha'i rgyal po bzo sbyangs gzugs can snying pos bcom
40b2(mdo sde2): ldan 'das dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po thams cad kyang dgra bcom pa/ zad pa zad pa/ bya ba byas pa/ byed pa byas pa// khur bor ba/ bdag gi don rjes su thob pa/ srid par

40b5(mdo sde2): rab brtan gyi smug ma'i nags khrod na bzhugs so// zhes thos so// thos nas kyang rgyal po'i 'byor pa chen po dang / rgyal po'i mthu chen pos shing rta nyi khri nyis stong dang / rta'i

40b7(mdo sde2): po'i khab nas byung ste/ de bzhin pas bzod pa'i sa ji srid du song nas/ bzhon pa las babs te rkang pa kho nas/ kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs nas/ yul ma ga d+ha'i rgyal po ba
40b8(mdo sde2): sbyangs gzugs can snying pos skabs gang nas/ bcom ldan 'das mthong ba'i bar skad der/ rgyal chos kyi mtshan ma lnga btsod pan dang / gdugs dang / ral gdugs
41a1(mdo sde2): dang / ral gri dang / rnga yang nor can dang / lham khra bo dag bud de bzhag go// de nas yul ma ga d+ha'i rgyal po bzo sbyangs gzugs can snying pos rgyal
41a2(mdo sde2): chos kyi mtshan ma lnga po dag phud de bzhag nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste phyin pa dang / bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar te/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa
41a3(mdo sde2): la btsugs nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud de/ btsun pa bdag ni yul ma ga d+ha'i rgyal po bzo sbyangs gzug can snying po lags so
41a4(mdo sde2): btsun pa bdag ni yul ma ga d+ha'i rgyal po bzo sbyangs gzugs can snying po lags so// rgyal po lags so zhes lan gsum gyi bar du rang gi ming rjes su sgrogs so//
41a5(mdo sde2): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rgyal po chen po de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ rgyal po chen po khyod ni yul ma ga d+ha'i rgyal po bzo sbyangs gzugs can snying po yin no//
41a6(mdo sde2): rgyal po chen po khyod ni yul ma ga d+ha'i rgyal po bzo sbyangs snying po yin no// rgyal po yin no// rgyal po chen po khyod rang gi stan gang yin pa la 'dug shig/ de nas yul ma ga
41a7(mdo sde2): d+ha'i rgyal po bzo sbyangs gzugs can snying pos/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug go// yul ma ga d+ha'i bram ze dang / khyi
41a8(mdo sde2): bdag kha gcig gis ni bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ phyogs cig tu 'khod do// kha gcig gis ni bcom ldan 'das la mngon gsum du phan/
41b1(mdo sde2): chun kun dga' ra bar 'gyur ba dang / yang dag par dga' bar 'gyur ba'i gtam sna tshogs dag gsol te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// kha cig gis ni bcom ldan 'das
41b2(mdo sde2): ga la ba de logs su thal ma sbyar te/ phyogs cig tu 'khod do// kha cig gis ni rgyang ring po nas bcom ldan 'das mthong nas/ cang mi smra bar phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i
41b3(mdo sde2): che ral pa can tshe dang ldan pa lte nga rgyas 'od srung 'khor de nyid du 'dus te 'dug par gyur to// de nas yul ma ga d+ha'i bram ze dang / mkhyim bdag rnams 'di snyam du sems te/
41b4(mdo sde2): ci dge sbyong chen po ral pa can lteng rgyas 'od srung gi drung du tshangs par spyad pa spyod dam/ 'on te ral pa can lteng rgyas 'od srungs nyid dge sbyong chen po'i spyan sngar tshangs
41b5(mdo sde2): par spyad pa spyod do// snyam mo// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi yul ma gau ta'i bram ze dang / khyim bdag rnams kyi sems thugs kyis mkhyen nas/ tshe dang ldan pa lteng
41b6(mdo sde2): rgyas 'od srung la tshigs su bcad pa'i dbyangs kyis dri ba dris pa/ lteng rgyas gnas pas 'di la ci mthong na// khyod kyis me spangs brtul zhugs kho la spyod/ khyed
41b7(mdo sde2): kyis ji ltar me'i sbyin sreg spangs// 'od srung de'i don ni de la spros// tshe dang ldan pa ldeng rgyas 'od srung gi gsol pa// 'di na kha cig zas dang skom dag dang /
41b8(mdo sde2): ro dang 'dod pa bud med brjod pa bgyid pa// rdzas byung de dag dri mar rang mthong bas// de skad mchod sbyin sreg la bdaga' mi dga'// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
42a1(mdo sde2): stsal pa// gal te khyod ni 'dod dang zas skom dang // de bzhin ro rnams dag la yid dga' bar mi byed na/ ji ltar lha mi'i 'jig rten dag la khyod kyi yid//
42a2(mdo sde2): dga' bar byed pa dris pa 'od gsung smros// tshe dang ldan pa lteng rgyas 'od srung gis gsol pa// go 'phang zhi mchog phung po ma mchis shig/ ci yang ma mchis 'dod srid
42a3(mdo sde2): ma chags la// mi 'gyur gzhan gyis mi dkri mthong lags pas// de slad mchod sbyin sred la bdag mi dga'// mi nyams go 'phang dam pa ma mthong tshe// mchod
42a4(mdo sde2): sbyin brtul zhugs rnams dang zhugs kyis kyang // grol bar 'gyur zhes bdag yid rmongs gyur cing / ldongs shig skyes shi'i rjes su zhugs par 'gyur// go'u
42a5(mdo sde2): tam skyes shing don tu rnam 'dren pa// thub pa bden pa'i rtsa la mnga' khyod byung zhing // gtso mchog skyob pas legs bshad da lta ni// go 'phang 'dus ma bgyid de bdag gis

42a8(mdo sde2): bas// ji ltar sems mnyam par gzhag pa bzhin du// bdag gis stan gyi steng na/ mi snang bar gyur pa de lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ shar/
42b1(mdo sde2): phyogs kyi steng gi nam mkha' la mngon par 'phags te/ spyod lam rnam pa bzhi po 'di lta ste/ 'chag pa dang / 'greng ba dang / 'dug pa dang / nyal ba dag byed do// me'i khams

61b3(mdo sde2): yang ngan song gsum du skye bar mi 'gyuraro// gzhon rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang gis sangs rgyas kyi zhing gang ga'i klung gi bye ma rnyed thams cad rin po che sna bdun gyis

61b7(mdo sde2): ba tshangs pa dang / rgyal po chen po bzhi dang / lha'i sras po mtshams rab dang / lha'i sras po dbang phyug chen pos bcom ldan 'das la lha rdzas kyi tsan dan gyi phye ma gtor to// mngon par ga

62a1(mdo sde2): deg ni/ lha dang mi dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis phyag bgyi ba'o// gdung bar bgyi ba'o// mchod par bgyi ba'o// chos kyi rnam grangs 'di su dag gi

62a5(mdo sde2): 'das kyis tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gsungs so// 'jig rten 'di dag gi/ mtshan ni gang gis bzung gyur pa// ma 'ongs pa'i dus na ni// de dag rkang gnyis mchog
